/y?YL
0 to 1 value controlling how much random offset is applied to each point. A value of 0 will generate a regular grid of points.
0 to 1 value indicating the amout of random offset that should be applied to the reguluarly spaced positions
0 to 1 value specifying the location on the local x-axis of the deformer around which the bend will occur. A value of 0 means the bend will occur around the minimum end of the deformer, a value of 1 means the bend will occur around the maximum end of the deformer, a value of 0.5 means the bend will occur at the center of the deformer volume.
0.0 to 1.0 value indicating the probability of this element being evaluated. Where a value of 0 means the element will never be evaluated and 1.0 means it will always be evaluated
